33rd-64th Decklists
===================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on August 28, 2016 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20170709072651im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/themes/wiz_mtg/images/global/generic-avatar-150.png)
By Frank Karsten and Marc Calderaro











We posted 9th - 32nd decklists [**here**](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gpind16/9-32-decklists-2016-08-28), but we know that you want even more!


Because Modern is such a deep format, here are the decklists of all remaining Top 64 competitors!


The following players scored 36 points (12-3).







#### Gabriel Palomino's Jeskai Harbinger – 33rd at GP Indianapolis 2016


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
